---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="629" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="633" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="641" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="653" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="657" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="662" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>
<a id="690" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">_</a> <a id="699" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png){: width="%50" }
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

  <a id="1862" class="Comment">-- Induction principle on paths</a>
  <a id="1896" class="Keyword">postulate</a>

## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

<a id="4529" class="Keyword">private</a>

In the following, we will need the following term:
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4817" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

### Lemma 2

- Action on paths of pairs

### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12139" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
<a id="neg"></a><a id="12147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12147" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="12151" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3017" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="12158" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3017" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="12165" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12147" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="12169" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a>  <a id="12175" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12177" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3053" class="InductiveConstructor">false</a>
